8.10. ~~**Backfill prisma/migrations file for ProspectVertical schema change + investigate Render deploy-chain.**~~ **CLOSED 2026-05-09 in v3.8.aax** (Sprint 44b atomic close). Sprint 44a Track 1 + Track 2 audit caught actual drift scope was **81 of 87 prod enums** plus their corresponding tables/columns — far beyond the original Item 8.10 ProspectVertical-only scope. v3.8.aa-dd (Apr 24 → May 4 window) shipped schema work via manual `prisma db push` to Neon, bypassing migration history entirely. Compounding root cause: Render Build Command lacked `prisma migrate deploy` step entirely, so the v3.8.ee `add_customer_approval_fields` migration that was authored + committed never applied via the deploy chain. **Fix shape (Sprint 44b atomic):** P1 — Render Build Command updated to canonical `npm install && npm run build && npx prisma migrate deploy && npx prisma migrate status --exit-code && cp -r src/assets dist/backend/src/assets`. P2 — baseline reset: `_prisma_migrations` ledger cleared on Neon, single `20260509170000_baseline_init` migration generated from `prisma migrate diff --from-empty --to-schema-datamodel` (3,652 lines, 87 enums, 120 tables) captures complete prod schema state, marked applied via `prisma migrate resolve --applied`. Prior 15 migrations archived to `backend/prisma/_archived_migrations_2026-05-09/` for posterity (NOT part of active chain). P3 — `prisma migrate status --exit-code` post-deploy gate fails build on any pending migrations (silent-skip class catch). P4 — single canonical schema mutation path doc at CLAUDE.md §2.2 + render.yaml + ci.yml comment all aligned in this commit (Pattern 6 spatial sub-mode contradiction resolved). PITR upgraded to 7 days (Neon Launch tier) before Phase 2 baseline reset for safety. **Sprint 44a Track 1 lesson:** initial grep on `ProspectVertical` returned correct empty result, but the conclusion "this is the only drift" was wrong — full audit needed direct `pg_type` + `information_schema` query (CSV of 87 enums) to surface complete scope. Pattern 6 sub-rule c candidate: "audits can be wrong" / verify prod-touching action against authoritative source before acting (queued for Sprint 44.5 §19 update). Original entry preserved below for history.

8.10-original. **Backfill prisma/migrations file for ProspectVertical schema change + investigate Render deploy-chain.** Surfaced 2026-05-04 during v3.8.v–v3.8.cc Lead Hunter sprint Step 4 verification. v3.8.aa (C4 commit [`6e2e6d9`](commit/6e2e6d9)) applied the `ProspectVertical` enum + `Customer.vertical` column via `prisma db push` directly to Neon. No migration file exists in [`backend/prisma/migrations/`](backend/prisma/migrations/). Production currently works because the live Neon DB matches the regenerated Prisma client — but a fresh DB clone (staging branch, dev workstation reset, disaster-recovery rebuild) will not pick up the enum + column from `migrate deploy` because there is no migration file to apply. **Risk profile: recovery-time gap, not runtime.** The Render `buildCommand` runs `npx prisma migrate deploy` on every deploy, which will be a no-op for this change because Neon already has it; the runtime `@prisma/client` is regenerated from the schema file and matches. Failure mode is invisible until someone resets a database from migrations alone, at which point the new enum + column will be missing and the type-system promise the client exports will diverge from the live schema. **Fix shape:** generate the missing migration file from the current schema diff using `npx prisma migrate diff --from-empty --to-schema-datamodel prisma/schema.prisma --script` (or against a baseline that excludes only the C4 change), place the resulting SQL in `backend/prisma/migrations/<timestamp>_add_prospect_vertical/migration.sql`, commit docs-only. **Test:** clone Neon to a staging branch, run `npx prisma migrate deploy` against it from scratch, confirm `ProspectVertical` enum exists and `customers.vertical` column exists with default `UNKNOWN`. Render's next prod build should be a no-op because Neon already has the schema. **Pairs with Items 8.6/8.7 audit hygiene** — both are recovery-time-gap issues that don't surface until you actually need to recover. Effort: small (~15-30 min including staging-clone test). Tracked here so the gap is closed in a dedicated mini-sprint, not silently absorbed. **Future-proofing:** the broader CLAUDE.md §2 directive to "avoid `prisma migrate dev`" because migration history has drift is itself a long-term risk; consolidating to a single baseline migration + going-forward migrate-deploy discipline is a separate architectural sprint outside Item 8.10's scope.

**Scope expansion 2026-05-05** — Item 8.10 was originally scoped to the v3.8.aa `db push` recovery-time gap (the `ProspectVertical` migration that was never authored). A separate but materially worse case surfaced during v3.8.oo verification: the Phase 3 (v3.8.ee, commit [`2fb5279`](commit/2fb5279), 2026-05-04) migration `20260504000000_add_customer_approval_fields` WAS authored, WAS committed, AND was NEVER applied to prod across ~24h and 9+ subsequent deploys (v3.8.ff through v3.8.oo). Track 1 diagnostic on 2026-05-05 confirmed: Query A returned zero rows for `customers.approved_at` + `customers.approved_by_id`; Query B returned zero rows in `_prisma_migrations` for any matching ledger entry. Manual `prisma migrate deploy` from local at 2026-05-05 17:35:00 UTC applied the migration cleanly in one step (post-DATABASE_URL-parity confirmation by Wasi + a Neon password rotation propagated to both Render env and local `.env`), demonstrating the migration itself was correct — failure was somewhere in Render's deploy chain. **Root-cause candidates to investigate (Phase 6 sprint):** (1) Render dashboard `buildCommand` drift from CLAUDE.md §2.2's documented spec — the dashboard is the SOT per §2.2 and `render.yaml` is cosmetic-only, so a manual edit could have weakened the chain; this is the most likely cause given §2.2 explicitly warns about this drift class. (2) `prisma migrate deploy` silently skipping or absent from the actual dashboard `buildCommand` (e.g. someone removed the `&& npx prisma migrate deploy` segment to work around an unrelated transient error and never restored it). (3) Build artifact cache holding a stale Prisma client that doesn't request the new columns at runtime, masking the drift until a query that actually needs the columns finally hits it. (4) Deploy chain runs migrate deploy but with a DATABASE_URL pointing at a different database than the runtime backend reads — would explain silent green builds with absent prod migrations; somewhat ruled out by the 2026-05-05 parity confirmation but worth a dashboard verification. **Fix surface:** (a) capture current dashboard `buildCommand` value as evidence, then re-align it with the documented value at CLAUDE.md §2.2 verbatim; (b) add a post-deploy schema-verify check that fails the build if `prisma migrate status` reports any pending migrations after `migrate deploy` ran (treats silent-skip as an explicit deploy failure rather than a transparent miss); (c) optional: periodic migration-drift cron (weekly) running `prisma migrate status` against prod and alerting `compliance@` on any pending migrations — captures drift even if it slips past a future deploy. **Effort:** medium sprint. Investigation step is ~30-60 min in Render dashboard + Render build log review for v3.8.oo's deploy. Fix steps are small but blocked on diagnosis. **Priority:** elevated — every future schema migration is at risk until this is closed. Pairs with the v3.8.aa migration backfill from the original Item 8.10 scope; both should land in the same sprint.

12.1. ~~**Accounting Console crash — `/accounting/analytics` null-toFixed.**~~ **CLOSED 2026-05-09 in v3.8.aau** (Sprint 41, scope expanded). Pattern 7 (catalogued Sprint 40c) `grep "marginPercent.*toFixed"` surfaced **4 unguarded crash sites**, not the 2 documented at logging time. Sprint 41 closes all four in one atomic per Sprint 39 Item 56 expansion precedent: `accounting/analytics:160`, `accounting/pnl:145` (Item 12.2), **`dashboard/finance:497` (NEW finding)**, **`dashboard/lane-analytics:366` (NEW finding)**. Em-dash fallback applied per audit recommendation (matches existing `/accounting/pnl:148` revenuePerMile pattern). Conditional class also null-guarded → neutral slate-400 instead of misleading red on null. Silent-NaN comparison fix bundled at `dashboard/finance:443-446` (`loads.filter((l) => l.marginPercent < 10)` was undercounting buckets when margin was null since NaN-coerce-false). `lane-analytics:127` reduce sum filtered to computed margins only. 12.1-original. **Accounting Console crash — `/accounting/analytics` null-toFixed.** Surfaced 2026-05-06 during v3.8.aab Sprint 24 smoke. Page renders full-screen "Something went wrong / Cannot read properties of null (reading 'toFixed')" error boundary, blocking AE Console analytics view entirely. Crash site: [`accounting/analytics/page.tsx:160`](frontend/src/app/accounting/analytics/page.tsx#L160) — `pct(l.marginPercent)` where the `pct` helper at line 10 is typed `(n: number) => string` and calls `.toFixed(1)` unconditionally. When any load row in the response has null `marginPercent` (likely when revenue=0 or cost=0 yields an undefined margin on the backend), the helper crashes. Same null-data crash class as 12.2. Severity: P1 — internal AE Console, full-page crash, blocks financial analysis surfacing. Sprint shape: paired with 12.2 below — single sprint covers both crash sites since root cause is shared (`Load.marginPercent` nullable + render code assumes non-null). Fix surface: (a) audit backend whether `marginPercent` should default to 0 or stay nullable; (b) if nullable, every UI render path must null-guard; recommend `(l.marginPercent ?? 0).toFixed(1)` or "—" em-dash fallback consistent with existing `revenuePerMile ? toFixed : "—"` pattern at [`pnl/page.tsx:148`](frontend/src/app/accounting/pnl/page.tsx#L148). Effort: ~20-40 lines across 2 files + decision on null-default vs em-dash. Single sprint.

12.2. ~~**Accounting Console crash — `/accounting/pnl` null-toFixed.**~~ **CLOSED 2026-05-09 in v3.8.aau** (Sprint 41). Original entry preserved below for history.

12.2-original. **Accounting Console crash — `/accounting/pnl` null-toFixed.** Surfaced 2026-05-06 during v3.8.aab Sprint 24 smoke. Same symptom as 12.1: full-screen "Cannot read properties of null (reading 'toFixed')" error boundary, blocking the Load P&L view. Crash site: [`accounting/pnl/page.tsx:145`](frontend/src/app/accounting/pnl/page.tsx#L145) — `load.marginPercent.toFixed(1)` with no null guard, inside the per-load row render. Note: same file at [`:148`](frontend/src/app/accounting/pnl/page.tsx#L148) DOES correctly null-guard `load.revenuePerMile` with the `?` ternary fallback to em-dash, so the pattern is established but inconsistently applied. KPI cards at [`:74-75`](frontend/src/app/accounting/pnl/page.tsx#L74) use `(data?.avgMarginPercent || 0).toFixed(1)` which is safe — the bug is only in the per-row table cell. Severity: P1, same as 12.1. **Bundles with 12.1** — single sprint covering both crash sites, since the fix is "audit `Load.marginPercent` nullability + apply the em-dash fallback pattern from line 148 to every render path." See 12.1 for sprint shape and effort estimate.

**Brand-token canonicalization residual (surfaced 2026-05-06 during Sprint 24a Phase A):**

30. **Residual `#C9A84C` (non-canonical olive-gold) refs in shipper components.** Surfaced 2026-05-06 during Sprint 24a (v3.8.aac) Phase A audit. 42. ~~**RC Modal Generate PDF + Send Tender buttons fail silently — quickPayFeePercent string-vs-number type mismatch.**~~ **CLOSED 2026-05-06 in v3.8.aam** (Sprint 34). Path β methodology cycle complete (Sprints 32 → 33 → 34) for the RC modal silent-fail class. **Cycle summary:** Sprint 32 (v3.8.aak) shipped error UI surfacing on all 3 RC handlers — silent error swallow class closed at observability layer. Sprint 33 (v3.8.aal) widened extractor to iterate Zod `details[]` array — generic "Validation error" banner became field-specific "Validation error — formData.X: <message>". Sprint 34 (v3.8.aam) shipped the targeted field fix once Sprint 33's extractor surfaced the specific rejection: `formData.quickPayFeePercent: Expected number, received string`. **Root cause:** [`RateConfirmationModal.tsx:188`](frontend/src/components/loads/RateConfirmationModal.tsx#L188) declares `quickPayFeePercent: string` in FormState (input ergonomics — three write paths all stringify via `String(...)`); backend Zod schema at [`validators/rateConfirmation.ts:117`](backend/src/validators/rateConfirmation.ts#L117) declares `z.number().optional()`. [`buildPayload()`](frontend/src/components/loads/RateConfirmationModal.tsx) spread `...form` carried the string unchanged — other numeric fields had explicit `parseFloat`/`parseInt`/`toNum` coercion before send, this one was the lone gap. **Fix shape — Path X1 (surgical buildPayload coercion):** added 3-line explicit coercion `quickPayFeePercent: form.quickPayFeePercent !== "" ? Number(form.quickPayFeePercent) : undefined`. **`!== ""` check preserves null-vs-zero distinction** (Phase A audit caught this): empty input → undefined → DB null (no value); explicit `"0"` → `Number(0)` = 0 → DB 0 (legitimate "no fee" STANDARD tier selection); `"1.5"` → 1.5 (correct). Alternative `Number(...) || undefined` rejected — would silently mask "0" as undefined, breaking STANDARD tier no-fee semantics. **Path X3 (`z.coerce.number()` validator change) rejected** per Phase A — changes validator semantics across schema, risks empty-string-to-zero confusion on other fields, belongs in §13.3 Item A28-2 architectural sprint. **Sweep result:** only `quickPayFeePercent` affected — single-field issue, not bug class. Other 10 `z.number()` validator fields are either explicitly coerced in buildPayload or not in payload at all. **Path β methodology validation:** ~38 LOC total across 3 atomic commits to retire 3 silently-broken handlers. Zero speculation, zero regressions. Error UI + widened extractor remain as PERMANENT diagnostic infrastructure for any future RC handler API failures. Pattern propagation candidate for other modals/forms across the codebase. **Item 45 logged (separate)** for follow-up cleanup of unvalidated payload fields. **Item A28-2 elevated** — today's cycle demonstrates the cost of "validator strict, frontend payload promiscuous" pattern; A28-2 architectural sprint (validator hardening via `z.preprocess` shape coercion at validator boundary) would prevent this class entirely; worth post-BKN priority bump from deferred queue. **Pre-commit verification:** backend `tsc --noEmit` clean (no backend changes), frontend `next build` clean. Net source change: 3 LOC (smallest hotfix shape). Per §3.1: v3.8.aal → v3.8.aam.

**Tender accept contract gaps (Phase A0 surfaced 2026-05-07, logged for sequential post-BKN sprints):**

51. **`notifyTenderAction` is dead code** ([notificationService.ts:91](backend/src/services/notificationService.ts#L91)). Function exists with proper `TENDER_ACCEPTED`/`DECLINED`/`COUNTERED`/`OFFERED` types + lane formatting + posterId fan-out, but **never called by any path** (grep: zero callers in `backend/src`). Direct accept uses manual `prisma.notification.create` with wrong `"LOAD_UPDATE"` type instead of `"TENDER_ACCEPTED"` ([tenderController.ts:127](backend/src/controllers/tenderController.ts#L127)). Waterfall accept skips notification entirely ([waterfallEngineService.ts:469](backend/src/services/waterfallEngineService.ts#L469) only fires SSE which has no consumer). **Fix shape:** wire `notifyTenderAction(tender.id, "ACCEPTED")` into both accept paths. ~5 LOC. **Sprint 37+ candidate.**

52. **Shipper tracking-link fan-out not fired on tender accept** ([shipperLoadNotifyService.ts:280](backend/src/services/shipperLoadNotifyService.ts#L280)). Comment claims it should fire on "waterfall accept, loadboard bid accept, direct tender accept" but only `loadBids.ts` + `orders.ts` call it. **Tender accept paths skip it** despite documented intent. Direct shipper not notified that their load was carrier-accepted; tracking link email never sent. **Fix shape:** wire `sendTrackingLinkToCrmContacts(load.id)` into both accept paths. ~6 LOC. **Sprint 37+ candidate.**

53. **Direct accept race condition (no transaction wrapper).** [`tenderController.acceptTender:80-94`](backend/src/controllers/tenderController.ts#L80) uses `Promise.all([...])` (concurrent, NOT atomic). v3.8.j docs claim "atomically sets carrierId + status=BOOKED in one transaction" but actual code isn't `prisma.$transaction`. Could leave inconsistent state if any of the 3 updates fails after others succeed (load updated to BOOKED but tender still OFFERED, or other tenders not declined). **Fix shape:** wrap in `prisma.$transaction([...])`. ~3 LOC. **Sprint 37+ candidate.**

54. **AE accept-on-behalf has no UI** (priority TBD). Backend [`acceptPosition`](backend/src/services/waterfallEngineService.ts#L403) (waterfall path) has NO user-id gate, AE could call it. [`acceptTender`](backend/src/controllers/tenderController.ts#L60) (direct path) blocks AE via `tender.carrier.userId !== req.user.id`. Either way, **zero AE UI exists** to invoke either path. Sprint 36 directive Step 3 "admin override" describes a flow that doesn't exist. **Priority decision pending Walk Step 2.5 BKN time-to-accept measurement** — if BKN reliably accepts in their portal, G5 stays backlog; if BKN is slow/unreliable, G5 elevates to Sprint 37 P0.

55. **`Load.status` divergence between accept paths — BOOKED vs DISPATCHED.** Direct accept ([tenderController.ts:87](backend/src/controllers/tenderController.ts#L87)) sets `status: "BOOKED"`. Waterfall accept ([waterfallEngineService.ts:443](backend/src/services/waterfallEngineService.ts#L443)) sets `status: "DISPATCHED"` (skips BOOKED entirely). Same conceptual event ("carrier accepts tender") → two different load lifecycle states. Public `/track` Sprint 27 mapping handles both ("Scheduled" for BOOKED-cluster, "Dispatched" for DISPATCHED) so customer-side is OK, but internal consistency is suspect. **Fix shape:** decide canonical, align both paths. ~5 LOC. **Sprint 37+ candidate.**

60. ~~**E2E seed extension for waterfall + loadbid bulk-path coverage.**~~ **CLOSED 2026-05-09 in v3.8.aaw** (Sprint 43, atomic with 62 + 66). 71. ~~**`(npx tsc || true)` suppresses TypeScript errors in build chain.**~~ **LOGGED + CLOSED 2026-05-10 in v3.8.abe** (Sprint 46). Root cause hypothesis from Sprint 44b Phase 3 was partially correct (the `|| true` did mask tsc errors) but Phase A audit at Sprint 46 revealed the deeper architectural cause: Render's env-level `NODE_ENV=production` (set in `render.yaml:34`) makes `npm install` skip the `devDependencies` block, leaving 12 declared `@types/*` packages uninstalled at build time. `Request` from `express` then resolves to `any`, `AuthRequest extends Request<any,any,any,any>` cascades, and tsc emits ~1,100 errors silenced by the `\|\| true`. Local CI uses `npm ci` (installs both deps + devDeps regardless of `NODE_ENV`) so CI tsc is clean — only Render diverged. **Empirical reproduction (Sprint 46 Phase B0 local sub-rule c gate):** `cd backend && rm -rf node_modules && NODE_ENV=production npm install && npm run build` produced exit code 0 with **1,398 error lines** (149 TS7016 + 907 TS2339 AuthRequest cascade + 63 TS7006 implicit any + 3 TS2503 Express namespace not found). Exact match to Sprint 45-RC Render build log. **Fix (3 changes, atomic):** (a) drop `\|\| true` from `backend/package.json:7` build script — strict tsc; (b) add `optionalDependencies` block with `@aws-sdk/client-rekognition ^3.1045.0` (Item 95, since we're touching package.json — biometricVerificationService.ts:9 has a try/catch dynamic require and was relying on the runtime-fail-graceful path); (c) add `NODE_ENV=development` prefix to Render dashboard buildCommand's `npm install` step — install-time only, runtime `NODE_ENV=production` preserved via render.yaml env block. **Architectural win:** build chain converted from fail-silent to fail-fast — tsc error → build halts → cp steps don't execute → deploy fails visibly. Sprint 45-RC's compass placeholder + Sprint 44b email signature fallback both shipped under fail-silent regime; Sprint 46 makes the next class of these visible in build logs immediately. **Sub-rule c lineage extends to 12 fires** in cumulative session arc (Sprint 46 audit-then-Phase-B0-gate counts as fire #11; fire #12 is the post-fix verification that landed clean). Per §3.1: v3.8.abd → v3.8.abe. **Items 95 + 96 closed alongside.**

95. ~~**`@aws-sdk/client-rekognition` referenced via dynamic require but not declared in package.json.**~~ **LOGGED + CLOSED 2026-05-10 in v3.8.abe** (Sprint 46 bundled with Item 71). [`backend/src/services/biometricVerificationService.ts:5-17`](backend/src/services/biometricVerificationService.ts#L5) wraps `require("@aws-sdk/client-rekognition")` in a try/catch gated by `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID` env. The runtime warning `[Biometric] AWS Rekognition SDK not available, using hash-based verification` is the intentional fallback path. But the module was referenced without being declared anywhere in `package.json` (not in `dependencies`, `devDependencies`, or `optionalDependencies`) — meaning even if `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID` were set, the require would still fail because npm never installed the package. Sprint 46 added `optionalDependencies` block: `{ "@aws-sdk/client-rekognition": "^3.1045.0" }`. Aligns with sibling `@aws-sdk/client-s3 ^3.998.0` major version. npm will try to install but won't fail if not available (graceful degradation matches the try/catch shape). When Wasi enables AWS biometric verification (set `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID` env), Rekognition path will actually be reachable. **Surfaced during Sprint 46 Phase A4 audit** — we were already touching package.json, so bundled atomically per §3.3.

99. ~~**`cp -r` POSIX nesting bug + sub-rule c gate extension (file-landed-at-expected-path verification).**~~ **LOGGED + CLOSED 2026-05-16 in v3.8.abf** (Sprint 47 atomic Item 99). Linux/POSIX `cp -r SRC DEST` semantics: when DEST already exists as a directory, SRC is copied as a CHILD of DEST → result `DEST/SRC_NAME/files...`. Only when DEST does not exist does cp create it with SRC's contents flat. `tsc` creates `dist/backend/src/{lib,config,assets}/` directories first (emitting compiled `.js` files into them), so by the time the buildCommand's cp steps run, all three destinations pre-exist → nesting fires silently. **Two retroactive production regressions explained:** (a) Sprint 44b Item 72 logged + closed `cp -r src/config dist/backend/src/config` step, but the file actually landed at `dist/backend/src/config/config/signatures/whaider.html` (nested). [`email/builder.ts:18`](backend/src/email/builder.ts#L18) reading `dist/backend/src/config/signatures/whaider.html` got "file not found" warning on every cold start since Sprint 44b. (b) Sprint 45-RC compass mark PNGs went to `dist/backend/src/lib/lib/srl_compass_*.png` (nested). Runtime `LOGO_DIR = __dirname` resolved to `dist/backend/src/lib/`, `resolveCompassPng()` returned null, placeholder navy ring fired on every Rate Confirmation PDF. Same single bug class, two visible failures. **Fix:** trailing-dot form `cp -r SRC/. DEST/` always copies CONTENTS regardless of whether DEST exists. Applied to all 3 cp commands in render.yaml + CLAUDE.md §2.2. **Empirical verification (Sprint 47 Phase B0 sub-rule c gate):** reproduced nesting locally + verified trailing-dot fix produces flat paths before commit. **Methodology principle banked (Item 99):** for file-producing build operations, "command exited 0" is necessary but NOT sufficient verification — must also verify file landed at expected runtime path. Sprint 44b Item 72 closure was technically incorrect: the cp command did run with exit 0, but the runtime path was never checked; the failure was invisible until Sprint 45-RC compass placeholder surfaced it 6+ days later. Sub-rule c gate extends: command-success verification + file-path verification. Pattern 6 sub-rule c fire #13 banks the extended gate for future build-chain sprints.

100. ~~**Skill canonical transit display unit — days → hours (broker industry standard drive-hour metric).**~~ **LOGGED + CLOSED 2026-05-16 in v3.8.abf** (Sprint 47 atomic Item 100). Sprint 45-RC's `drawLaneEconomics` rendered transit as `${transitDays.toFixed(1)} days` (hardcoded). Pre-Sprint-47 RC PDF for 1,352-mile lane showed "2.7 days" (from `miles / 500` solo HOS pacing). Technically correct math but UX-poor — carriers convert mentally to drive hours regardless because HOS log entries, ETA windows, and dispatch conversations all run in hours. Per broker industry survey (TQL/Convoy/Uber Freight rate cons reviewed during Sprint 47 Phase A): every major broker's lane economics widget uses hours, not days. **Fix:** added optional `transitUnit: "hours" | "days" = "hours"` parameter to `drawLaneEconomics` in [`backend/src/lib/srl-chrome.ts`](backend/src/lib/srl-chrome.ts) (default "hours" per Sprint 47 D3); RC generator in [`pdfService.ts`](backend/src/services/pdfService.ts) now computes `transitHours = miles / 55` (industry-standard 55 mph highway average) and passes `"hours"`. Display: "24.6 hrs" for the same 1,352-mile lane. **Days path preserved** for any future caller that wants calendar-day display (multi-day plan, HOS-strict pacing). Skill `srl_chrome.ts` upstream sync recommended at next skill update — current change is local-only mirror of skill canonical.

101. ~~**Skill font registration in `srl-chrome.ts` mirroring BOL v2.9 pattern.**~~ **LOGGED + CLOSED 2026-05-16 in v3.8.abf** (Sprint 47 atomic Item 101). Sprint 45-RC's RC PDF rendered in Helvetica + Times-Bold (PDFKit built-ins), diverging from BOL v2.9's Playfair Display + DM Sans (skill canonical per `tokens.md`). User-visible inconsistency: BOL and RC are sibling shipping documents but used different font stacks. **Root cause:** `backend/src/lib/srl-chrome.ts:76-81` hardcoded PDFKit built-in font names (`Helvetica`, `Times-Bold`, etc.) for portability — the skill chrome was authored to work without registering custom TTFs. But in this monorepo, TTFs already ship at `backend/src/assets/fonts/bol-v2.9/` (9 files: 4 Playfair + 5 DMSans variants) from the Sprint v3.8.b BOL v2.9 epic. **Fix:** (a) updated FONT_* constants to skill canonical names (`Playfair-Bold`, `DMSans-Regular`, etc.); (b) added exported `registerSkillFonts(doc)` function mirroring `generateBOLFromLoad` registration pattern at `pdfService.ts:317-326`; (c) RC generator in `generateEnhancedRateConfirmation` now invokes `registerSkillFonts(doc)` immediately after `new PDFDocument(...)`. Without the registration call, fontkit throws "Font not found" on first text() invocation. **Courier-Bold preserved** (PDFKit built-in mono — skill spec doesn't include a custom monospace; kept for reference fields like load IDs + TRACK label per `pdf-chrome.md`). **Ligature suppression** — Sprint v3.8.b Option β monkey-patch at `pdfService.ts:197-265` prevents fontkit ligature substitution (`classified → classifed` bug). If RC PDF renders italic Playfair with ligature artifacts post-Sprint-47, same monkey-patch approach migrates into `srl-chrome.ts` as a separate hotfix; deferred unless surfaces visually.

103. ~~**Fontkit ligature substitution bug — "Rate Confirmation" rendered as "Rate Confrmation" post-Sprint-47.**~~ **LOGGED + CLOSED 2026-05-16 in v3.8.abg** (Sprint 47.b atomic Item 103). Sprint 47 visual verification post-deploy surfaced the bug exactly as the Sprint 47 commit message predicted ("deferred unless surfaces visually"). 3 of 4 "Rate Confirmation" instances rendered with the `fi` glyph substitution that truncates the `i` — affecting Playfair-Bold 22pt H1 display, DMSans-Regular 8pt continuation header, and DMSans-Italic 7.5pt CARRIER · ACCEPTANCE body. Only the legacy Helvetica T&C body rendered correctly because PDFKit built-in fonts have no fontkit ligature substitution. **Root cause:** same fontkit `liga`/`clig`/`rlig`/`dlig` OpenType feature substitution Sprint v3.8.b Option β monkey-patch fixed for BOL v2.9 (classified → classifed bug). Sprint 47 added skill canonical font registration (`registerSkillFonts(doc)`) but didn't port the monkey-patch — explicitly documented as "deferred unless surfaces visually" in Sprint 47 commit. **Fix:** ported the canonical monkey-patch verbatim from [`pdfService.ts:248-297`](backend/src/services/pdfService.ts#L248) into the END of `registerSkillFonts(doc)` in [`backend/src/lib/srl-chrome.ts:119+`](backend/src/lib/srl-chrome.ts#L119). Bundled with font registration — every skill-chrome consumer that calls `registerSkillFonts(doc)` now inherits BOTH font registration AND ligature suppression in one call. Future Sprint 45-RC2 (Invoice) + 45-RC3 (Settlement) migrations auto-benefit. Monkey-patch disables 4 OpenType ligature features (`liga`/`clig`/`rlig`/`dlig`) while preserving `kern: true` for proper typography. Exact-shape verbatim port verified Phase B0 sub-rule c gate. **Phase B1 sub-rule c gate D4:** local PDF smoke test generated post-fix RC PDF via direct service call; pdf-parse text extraction verified all 4 "Rate Confirmation" instances render with the dot on `i`. Empirical proof BEFORE commit + push. Net source change: ~50 LOC in `srl-chrome.ts`. CLOSED in Sprint 47.b.

104. ~~**T&C body + 3 coupled Helvetica references in `generateEnhancedRateConfirmation` swapped to FONT_BODY/FONT_BODY_BOLD skill canonical.**~~ **LOGGED + CLOSED 2026-05-16 in v3.8.abg** (Sprint 47.b atomic Item 104 bundled with Item 103). Original directive scope was T&C body (1 line: `doc.font("Helvetica", 7.5)` at line 1567). Scope EXPANDED to 4 Helvetica references during Phase B0 audit because (a) `heightOfString(text)` measurement at line 1526 must use the same font as text rendering at line 1540 to produce a correctly-sized panel — coupled pair must migrate together; (b) T&C section label at line 1549 (`Helvetica-Bold 7pt`) paired with body at line 1567 for visual consistency — splitting them would render T&C header in Helvetica-Bold and body in DMSans, introducing a NEW visual inconsistency worse than Sprint 47 baseline; (c) all 4 references are in the same generator function + same atomic commit per §3.3. Plus added `export` keyword to `FONT_BODY` + `FONT_BODY_BOLD` constants in srl-chrome.ts (were `const` before, not exported); imported in pdfService.ts. **Safe post-Item-103 monkey-patch** — DMSans fonts are precisely the fonts that exhibited the ligature substitution bug Item 103 fixed; without the monkey-patch port, Item 104's swap would have introduced new ligature artifacts on the previously-clean Helvetica T&C body. Items 103 + 104 must ship atomically; deploying 104 without 103 would be a regression. 105. ~~**Pattern 6 sub-rule c — "deferred-but-not-missed" protocol canonical (named sub-pattern).**~~ **LOGGED + CLOSED 2026-05-16 in v3.8.abg** (Sprint 47.b methodology meta-finding). Sprint 47's commit message explicitly documented the deferred ligature risk verbatim: *"Ligature suppression — Sprint v3.8.b Option β monkey-patch... if RC PDF renders italic Playfair with ligature artifacts post-Sprint-47, same monkey-patch approach migrates into srl-chrome.ts as a separate hotfix; deferred unless surfaces visually."* When the risk surfaced via Wasi's visual verification of the post-Sprint-47 RC PDF, Sprint 47.b activated exactly per that documented plan — single-day turnaround from surface → atomic fix → push. **This is NOT a sub-rule c miss.** Sprint 47 didn't have the data to know the ligature would visibly surface (could have been correctly rendered by Playfair's specific `fi` glyph; fontkit ligature behavior varies by font's OpenType tables). Documenting the deferred risk as a known-conditional follow-up sprint, with explicit activation criteria, is the gate's INTENDED deferral protocol. Sub-rule c fire count holds at 13 — deferred-but-not-missed is a sub-pattern, not a fire. **Methodology principle banked:** when a sprint identifies a downstream risk it can't empirically validate at commit time (e.g., visual rendering that needs production-equivalent deployment), document the risk + activation criteria + planned hotfix path in the commit message. Future sprints have a clear handoff if the risk materializes. The protocol works as designed when (a) Sprint N flags the risk explicitly, (b) Sprint N+1 activates immediately when verification surfaces it. §19 quarterly meta-commit candidate alongside Item 96 (fail-fast vs fail-silent) and Item 99 (runtime-path verification gate extension). Sub-rule c now has THREE named methodology principles: authoritative-source-verification (canonical), fail-fast-build-chain (Item 96), runtime-path-verification (Item 99), AND deferred-but-not-missed (Item 105). All four are §19 case studies for next quarterly review.

102. ~~**`drawPartiesBlock` y-coordinate overlap with meta strip date row.**~~ **LOGGED + CLOSED 2026-05-16 in v3.8.abf** (Sprint 47 atomic Item 102). Sprint 45-RC PDF rendered "May 16, 2026PARTIES" as visible overlap on page 1 — the meta strip's DATE value row collided with the `drawPartiesBlock` PARTIES small-caps label sitting `y - 14` above the panels. Root cause: in [`pdfService.ts:1414`](backend/src/services/pdfService.ts#L1414) the RC generator called `drawPartiesBlock(..., y - 4)`; `drawMetaStrip` returns y at meta strip's bottom edge, and `drawPartiesBlock` internally subtracts 14 from the passed `yTop` to position its PARTIES label, so the effective label y was `metaStripBottom - 4 - 14 = metaStripBottom - 18`, which fell INSIDE the meta strip's value row. **Fix:** bumped y-offset from `y - 4` to `y + 12` — gives the parties label clearance from the meta strip row above. Visually verified via local rebuild + Wasi pixel verification on Phase 4 post-deploy.

96. ~~**Architectural lesson — build chain fail-fast vs fail-silent as canonical methodology principle.**~~ **LOGGED + CLOSED 2026-05-10 in v3.8.abe** (Sprint 46 meta-finding). Pre-Sprint-46 backend build chain: `npm install (NODE_ENV=production skips devDeps) → (npx tsc \|\| true) (mask errors) → cp -r src/assets/config/lib (succeeds unconditionally) → prisma migrate deploy → deploy succeeds with broken artifacts`. Net effect: TWO classes of regression silently shipped to production over the past sprint arc — (1) Sprint 44b email signature template `dist/backend/src/config/signatures/whaider.html` missing (caught by Sprint 44b Item 72 pre-commit grep audit, fixed by adding `cp -r src/config` step — but the underlying fail-silent build chain wasn't addressed); (2) Sprint 45-RC compass mark PNGs `dist/backend/src/lib/srl_compass_*.png` missing despite buildCommand including `cp -r src/lib` step — the cp didn't fail, the `tsc` step "passed" (via `\|\| true`), so the deploy went through with broken assets; user saw placeholder navy ring instead of canonical SRL compass mark. **Post-Sprint-46 build chain is fail-fast:** tsc errors → npm run build exits non-zero → cp steps don't run → deploy halts with visible failure. Future Sprint-44b/45-RC class regressions become impossible at the architectural level rather than requiring per-incident pre-commit grep audits. **Methodology principle:** silent-success is worse than loud-failure on prod deploy chains because (a) silent-success normalizes ignoring the build log noise, (b) the failure mode propagates to runtime where it's harder to diagnose, (c) eventually shipping a "live" service that's missing assets damages user trust. Banking for §19 quarterly meta-commit as canonical methodology principle. **Item 96 LOG + CLOSE** — the principle is now documented at CLAUDE.md §2.2 + permanently embedded in the post-Sprint-46 build chain itself.

Pairs with the waterfall expirationMinutes input — could ship as a small consolidation sprint. **Sprint 46+ candidate.** Not BKN-blocking — 24h default is the broker-industry standard and matches what the platform shipped through Sprint 44d.

90. **`LoadTender` schema has no `declineReason` field — `sendTenderDeclinedEmail` always passes `undefined`.** Surfaced 2026-05-10 during Sprint 45a Sub-phase 3 implementation when the directive's `tender.declineReason ?? undefined` reference was checked against the actual schema (Pattern 6 sub-rule c). [`schema.prisma:1338-1360`](backend/prisma/schema.prisma#L1338) `model LoadTender` has fields {id, loadId, carrierId, status, offeredRate, counterRate, respondedAt, expiresAt, createdAt, deletedAt, waterfallPositionId} — NO `declineReason`. The `declineReason` field at line 1441 lives on `WaterfallPosition` (waterfall-tender position decline tracking); the line 4265 instance lives on `CarrierCallLog` (outbound call log outcomes). Neither is `LoadTender`. The [`declineTender` controller](backend/src/controllers/tenderController.ts) at line 314 doesn't capture a reason — it only sets `status: "DECLINED"` + `respondedAt`. **Net effect today:** `sendTenderDeclinedEmail`'s `declineReason` parameter is always undefined; the conditional rendering (D4 ratification) gracefully handles by omitting the row. AE-facing email reads "Tender declined by {carrier}" with no reason context. **Sprint shape:** Sprint 46+ candidate. Add `declineReason String?` to `LoadTender` model + schema migration; extend `declineTender` controller to read `req.body.reason` (~5 LOC); extend frontend decline UI (carrier portal `/carrier/dashboard/tenders` decline modal) to capture reason — categorized dropdown per the brainstorm earlier (Rate too low, Capacity full, Lane mismatch, Equipment unavailable, Other) + free-text fallback. ~80-120 LOC across 4 files. Pairs naturally with Sprint 45b counter-tender email (Item 89) since both involve carrier-side response capture. Not BKN-blocking — reasons feed analytics + email body context, not core flow.

46. ~~**RC Modal `fuelSurchargeType` enum mismatch — frontend `PER_MILE` vs backend `FLAT|PERCENTAGE`.**~~ **CLOSED 2026-05-07 in v3.8.aan** (Sprint 35). Expected 'FLAT' | 'PERCENTAGE', received 'PER_MILE'` on next Generate PDF attempt after Sprint 34 closed `quickPayFeePercent`. **Triple-source disagreement** found at Phase A: Frontend FormState (line 182) `"FLAT" \| "PER_MILE"` vs Frontend SelectField (line 1828) `PER_MILE` option vs Backend Zod validator ([line 106](backend/src/validators/rateConfirmation.ts#L106)) `["FLAT", "PERCENTAGE"]` vs Backend Prisma enum ([schema.prisma:446](backend/prisma/schema.prisma#L446)) `FLAT/PERCENTAGE`. **Origin — domain concept conflation:** Backend validator [line 104](backend/src/validators/rateConfirmation.ts#L104) has `rateType: z.enum(["FLAT", "PER_MILE"])` — different field, different concept. Frontend RC modal copy-pasted `PER_MILE` from rateType to fuelSurchargeType. Industry-standard distinction: "per mile" rates apply to base load rate (rateType); "percentage" surcharges apply to fuel only (fuelSurchargeType). **Fix — Path A (frontend aligns to backend canonical):** FormState type union `PER_MILE → PERCENTAGE`; SelectField onChange cast and option both `PER_MILE → PERCENTAGE` (label "Per Mile" → "Percentage"). Plus `initForm` defensive normalization coerces any legacy stored `PER_MILE` to `FLAT` default. ~5 LOC source + 3 LOC normalize. **Path B (add PER_MILE to backend enum) rejected** — would cement frontend's domain conflation. Backend canonical `FLAT/PERCENTAGE` is correct per industry convention. **Pre-commit verification:** backend `tsc --noEmit` clean (no backend changes), frontend `next build` clean. Per §3.1: v3.8.aam → v3.8.aan.

47. **Frontend `Stop.type` enum declares `"STOP"` value not allowed by validator.** Surfaced 2026-05-07 during Sprint 35 Phase A enum sweep. Recommend **align frontend to backend** since STOP isn't industry-standard for ABL multi-stop routing (always PICKUP or DELIVERY at every stop). ~3 LOC fix when prioritized. Post-BKN cleanup. 93. **Pattern 6 sub-rule c — pixel-verification-as-audit-gate observation.** Surfaced 2026-05-10 during Sprint 45-RC Phase A2 PDF capture. Phase A Track 1 audit produced 7 RC PDF findings via code-side analysis (read pdfService.ts, compared against skill canonical, traced data shapes). Phase A2 pixel verification (open the PDF, look at it) surfaced an 8th finding the code audit predicted nothing about: rate breakdown rendered to page 4 instead of page 1. The cause was `checkPageBreak` thresholds + section-ordering interaction that produced visible-but-non-obvious pagination behavior — invisible from grepping section names; visible only when looking at the rendered output. **Methodology lesson:** code-side audits are authoritative for code contracts (function signatures, type shapes, control flow) but NOT for visual contracts (which-page-does-X-render-on, what-does-the-rendered-pixel-density-feel-like, where-does-an-AE-eye-fall-first). Visual audits require visual capture — there's no shortcut via grep, AST parsing, or static type inspection. Code-side audit answers "what could it render?"; pixel verification answers "what does it render?". The two are complementary, not substitutable. **Sprint shape:** docs-only meta-commit candidate at next quarterly §19 review. Add to §19 Pattern 6 sub-rule c body as a NEW sub-class — pixel-verification-as-audit-gate distinct from authoritative-source-verification. Lineage: cumulative arc sub-rule c fire count post-Sprint-45-RC = 9, with Phase A2 (this finding) + Phase B Sub-phase 3 (package.json directive correction) being fires 8 + 9. **Item 93 LOG OPEN** — closure deferred until quarterly §19 review or Sprint 44.5-style methodology meta-commit appends the case-study addendum.

94. **`drawPanel` single-line `lineBreak: false` limitation surfaced during Sprint 45-RC RC migration.** Surfaced 2026-05-10 during Sprint 45-RC Phase B Sub-phase 2 implementation. Skill `srl-chrome.ts` `drawPanel` (line 667) renders `bodyText` with `lineBreak: false` — single-line only, no wrapping. For Rate Confirmation Special Instructions which can be multi-paragraph free-text, `drawPanel` is insufficient. **Workaround in Sprint 45-RC:** `generateEnhancedRateConfirmation` renders the cream-2 frame manually (using `doc.roundedRect.fillAndStroke`) + the body text with `width: CONTENT_W - 20, lineGap: 1` for proper wrapping. Same outcome visually as `drawPanel` would produce IF it supported wrapping. **Skill upstream fix:** `drawPanel` should accept a `wrap?: boolean` option (default false to preserve existing single-line callers) that switches `lineBreak: false` → text wrapping with measured panel height. ~10 LOC fix in `srl-chrome.ts`. When implemented, mirror the change into `backend/src/lib/srl-chrome.ts` (the per-skill manual-sync rule still applies). **Sprint shape:** skill-side fix at next skill update; backend mirror at next manual sync. Not BKN-blocking — Sprint 45-RC's manual workaround produces equivalent visual output today.

45. **RC Modal payload spread includes fields not declared in validator (`totalCarrierPay`, `netPayAmount`).** Surfaced 2026-05-06 during Sprint 34 Phase A. [`RateConfirmationModal.tsx`](frontend/src/components/loads/RateConfirmationModal.tsx) `buildPayload()` does `...form` spread which includes `totalCarrierPay` (FormState line 184) and `netPayAmount` (line 189). Backend validator [`createRateConfirmationSchema`](backend/src/validators/rateConfirmation.ts) does NOT declare these fields. Zod's default behavior is `.strip()` — unknown keys are silently dropped from the parsed output without raising validation errors. **No current bug** — fields are silently discarded server-side. **Cleanup options:** (a) remove from `...form` spread by reshaping payload to explicitly-listed fields only; (b) add the two fields to the validator schema if useful for backend (e.g., for analytics/audit); (c) change validator to `.strict()` to fail-loud on unknown keys. **Sprint shape:** small (~5 LOC) but architectural decision — option (a) is cleanest for forward compatibility, option (c) catches future drift but requires payload audit across all RC consumers. **NOT in Sprint 34 scope** per §3.3 atomic-commit rule — Sprint 34 stayed atomic on Item 42 closure. **Priority:** low. No load is currently broken. Pairs naturally with §13.3 Item A28-2 (validator hardening) post-BKN.

43. ~~**Silent error swallow on RC modal handlers — handleSaveDraft / handleGeneratePdf / handleSendTender catch blocks all `console.error` only with no UI feedback.**~~ **CLOSED 2026-05-06 in v3.8.aak** (Sprint 32 Path β). Bug class: "API failures invisible to user." Surfaced as a side-effect of Item 42 audit — even if Item 42 is fixed, future API failures on these handlers would silently fail the same way. Same defensive class as Sprint 26b error boundary patterns. **Fix:** added `submitError: string | null` state to RC modal root component; new `extractErrorMessage(err, fallback)` helper checks `err.response.data.error → .message → err.message → fallback` (handles axios + native Error + plain string shapes); all 3 handlers reset error to null at start, set error in catch block on failure; new JSX banner above button row conditionally rendered when `submitError` set — `bg-red-50 border-l-4 border-red-500 text-red-700` (canonical Tailwind error palette, works on cream + dark contexts) with "Error:" label prefix. Banner auto-dismisses on next handler attempt (resets at handler start). **Future API failures on these handlers self-diagnose via screenshot** — no DevTools workflow required. ~25 LOC (state + helper + 3 handler edits + JSX banner). **Pattern propagation candidate:** other modals/forms across the codebase likely have the same silent-error class; could roll up into a typing-discipline / observability sprint to apply pattern consistently. Not in Sprint 32 scope per §3.3 atomic-commit rule.

**RC Modal carrier search route fix — hotfix (logged + closed 2026-05-06 in v3.8.aaj, Sprint 31):**

39. ~~**RC Modal carrier search returns 404 silent-fail (B28-T1.3-A re-diagnosed).**~~ **CLOSED 2026-05-06 in v3.8.aaj** (Sprint 31). Originally walked as "P1 missing empty state on carrier search." Phase A audit corrected the diagnosis — the empty state was never the bug. Root cause: [`RateConfirmationModal.tsx:1422`](frontend/src/components/loads/RateConfirmationModal.tsx#L1422) (pre-fix) called `api.get("/carriers/all", ...)` but the canonical handler `getAllCarriers` is mounted at `/api/carrier/all` (singular) per [`backend/src/routes/carrier.ts:123`](backend/src/routes/carrier.ts#L123), NOT `/api/carriers/all` (plural). The plural route file defines `GET /` (with validation) and `GET /:id`, so Express matched `/api/carriers/all` against the `/:id` route with `req.params.id = "all"`, called `getCarrierDetail("all")` → returned 404. Frontend `useQuery` silently swallowed the 404, `data` stayed undefined, dropdown render gated on `showSearch && carriers && (...)` never fired — AE saw silent dead-state (input typed, no dropdown, no error, no autofill). **Re-diagnosis pattern matches Sprint 26 → 26b** (accessorial walk surfaced symptom, audit identified actual root cause): walk surfaces what user sees, audit identifies real bug class, correct fix ships. Memory #11 firing again. **Fix:** 1-character change — removed `s` from `carriers/all`. New URL `/carrier/all` now resolves to the actual `getAllCarriers` handler. Inline comment added at the call site referencing Sprint 31 + Item 40 (the duplicate-route consolidation backlog). **Pre-commit verification:** backend `tsc --noEmit` clean (no backend changes), frontend `next build` clean. Net LOC change: ~7 (1 URL char swap + 6-line inline comment). Per §3.1: v3.8.aai → v3.8.aaj.

40. **Duplicate carrier-route definitions: `routes/carrier.ts` (singular) vs `routes/carriers.ts` (plural).** Surfaced 2026-05-06 during Sprint 31 Phase A audit. Two backend files define routes for the same `getAllCarriers` controller at different URL paths with different validation: [`backend/src/routes/carrier.ts:123`](backend/src/routes/carrier.ts#L123) `GET /all` (NO validation, accepts arbitrary query params); [`backend/src/routes/carriers.ts:102`](backend/src/routes/carriers.ts#L102) `GET /` (WITH `validateQuery(carrierQuerySchema)`). Both call the same controller. Result: validation drift between `/api/carrier/all?search=X` (anything goes) and `/api/carriers?search=X` (must match Zod schema). Multiple frontend callers may hit either path. The plural route also defines `GET /:id` (`getCarrierDetail`) which is the silent-trap that caused Item 39's 404. **Sprint shape:** consolidate to one route file + one URL pattern. Recommend keeping the plural `/api/carriers` (REST convention for collection) with proper sub-paths: `GET /` (list), `GET /search` or `GET /?search=X` (search), `GET /:id` (detail). Migrate all frontend callers. Delete the singular file. Validation lives at the canonical path. **Effort:** medium — requires grep across `frontend/src/` for all `api.get("/carrier/...")` and `api.get("/carriers/...")` callers, decision on canonical paths, route file consolidation, then frontend updates. ~30-50 LOC across 5-10 files. **Out of Sprint 31 scope** per §3.3 "no scope creep" — Sprint 31 atomic on the silent-fail URL fix only. **Tracked for post-BKN architecture queue** per locked sprint sequencing.
